Everyone can join the team, with or without prior experience.</p><p id="65e8" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mg mh gu mi b mj mk ml mm mn mo mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd gn bk">They were a popular team, having also some customs songs made for them (In Russian).</p><figure class="nh ni nj nk nl nm"><div class="pg ph l fj"><div class="pi pj l"></div></div></figure><figure class="nh ni nj nk nl nm"><div class="pg ph l fj"><div class="pi pj l"></div></div></figure><p id="f115" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mg mh gu mi b mj mk ml mm mn mo mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd gn bk">Amnesia was banned from Zelenka at October 29, 2023.
